`source/common/router/config_impl.cc` - Implementation of route matching algorithm\\n\\n**Key Classes and Their Roles:**\\n\\n#### 1. **ConfigImpl** (overall route configuration wrapper)\\n   - - Uses lowest-cost-first matching: exact > prefix wildcards > suffix wildcards > default\\n   - **Route matching dispatch** (lines 2161-2171):\\n     - `RouteMatcher::route()`: Finds virtual host,
